      'pinning"), the common helper for allocating and preparing a folio in the\r\n' +

      'swapin on device B, and VMA readahead tries to read swap entries from\r\n' +
      "device A.  It's not easy to trigger, but in theory, it could cause real\r\n" +
      'issues.\r\n' +

    title: 'CVE-2025-40271 In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'fs/proc fix uaf in proc_readdi...',
    link: 'https//nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2025-40271',
    pubDate: 'Sat, 06 Dec 2025 22:15:00 GMT',
    content: '![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[![CDATA[In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'fs/proc fix uaf in proc_readdir_de()\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'Pde is erased from subdir rbtree through rb_erase(), but not set the node\r\n' +
      'to EMPTY, which may result in uaf access.  We should use RB_CLEAR_NODE()\r\n' +
      'set the erased node to EMPTY, then pde_subdir_next() will return NULL to\r\n' +
      'avoid uaf access.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'We found an uaf issue while using stress-ng testing, need to run testcase\r\n' +
      'getdent and tun in the same time.  The steps of the issue is as follows\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '1) use getdent to traverse dir /proc/pid/net/dev_snmp6/, and current\r\n' +
      '   pde is tun3\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '2) in the [time windows] unregister netdevice tun3 and tun2, and erase\r\n' +
      '   them from rbtree.  erase tun3 first, and then erase tun2.  the\r\n' +
      '   pde(tun2) will be released to slab\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '3) continue to getdent process, then pde_subdir_next() will return\r\n' +
      '   pde(tun2) which is released, it will case uaf access.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'CPU 0                                      |    CPU 1\r\n' +
      '-------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n' +
      'traverse dir /proc/pid/net/dev_snmp6/      |   unregister_netdevice(tun->dev)   //tun3 tun2\r\n' +
      'sys_getdents64()                           |\r\n' +
      '  iterate_dir()                            |\r\n' +
      '    proc_readdir()                         |\r\n' +
      '      proc_readdir_de()                    |     snmp6_unregister_dev()\r\n' +
      '        pde_get(de)                       |       proc_remove()\r\n' +
      '        read_unlock(proc_subdir_lock)    |         remove_proc_subtree()\r\n' +
      '                                           |           write_lock(proc_subdir_lock)\r\n' +
      '        [time window]                      |           rb_erase(root->subdir_node, parent->subdir)\r\n' +
      '                                           |           write_unlock(proc_subdir_lock)\r\n' +
      '        read_lock(proc_subdir_lock)      |\r\n' +
      '        next = pde_subdir_next(de)        |\r\n' +
      '        pde_put(de)                       |\r\n' +
      '        de = next    //UAF                |\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'rbtree of dev_snmp6\r\n' +

      'allocator again before it is placed back in the direct mapping.\r\n' +

      'kernel tries to access it via the direct map, it would result in a\r\n' +
